   Bhāgirasi ma     se   Pabhūtā bhimavantato the   Titthassa the   Padumuttaranāyako sambuddho dipaduttemo ma     a   Gaṅgātiramupāgato ma the   Nāvālañachakaṃ     se the a   Tāraṇo the se a   Vipasastithe   Jhānanirataṃ the    Jhāyinaṃ bhikkhunaṃ the  imā dve gāthā     se petthakesu na vijjanti 
  
                  
  
    Ānandattharāpadānaṃ 
  
     Ārāmadvārā nikkhamma padumuttaro mahāmuni 
 Vassento   amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ nibbāpesi mahājanaṃ 
  
     Satasahassā te vīrā   chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā 
 Parivārenti sambuddhaṃ chāyāva anapāyini   
  
     Hatthikkhandhāgato āsiṃ setacchattaṃ varuttamaṃ 
 Sucārurūpaṃ disvāna vitti me upapajjatha 
  
     Oruyha hatthikkhandhamhā upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Ratanāmayachattaṃ me buddhaseṭṭhassa dhārayiṃ 
  
                  
  
     Mama saṅkappamaññāya padumuttaro mahāisi 
 Taṃ kathaṃ ṭhapayitvāna imā gathā abhāsata 
  
      Yo so chattaṃ adhāresi soṇṇālaṅkārabhusitaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhasato 
  
     Ito gantvā ayaṃ poso tusitaṃ āvasissati 
 Anubhossati sampattiṃ accharāhi purakkhato 
  
     Catuntiṃsanikkhantuñca devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Balādhipo aṭṭhasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
  
     Aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ mabhiyā kārayissati 
  
     Kappasatasahassamhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena   satthā leke bhavissati 
  
     Sakyānaṃ kulaketussa cātibandhu bhavissati 
 Ānando nāma nāmena upaṭṭhāko mahesino 
  
     Ātāpi nipako cāpi   bāhusaccesu kovido 
 Nivātavutti atthaddho sabbapāṭhi bhavissati 
  
     Padhānapahitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo  
  
     Santi āraññakā nāgā kuñajarā saṭṭhihāyanā 
 Nidhā pabhinnamātaṅgā īsādantā urūḷhavā 
  
     Anekasatasahassā paṇḍitāpi mahiddhikā 
 Sabbe te buddhanāgassa na hontupanidhimbhi te   
  
   Vassanto ma       Satasahassāni virā       Anupāyini ma the   Nāmena the   Saddho the   Honti paṇidimbhi ma na honta parivimbhitā     
  
                  
  
     Ādiyāme namassāmi majjhime atha pacchime 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ 
  
     Ātāpi nipako cāpi sampajāno patissato 
 Sotāpattiphalampatto sekkhabhumisu kovido 
  
     Tappeto satasahasse yaṃ kammamabhinihariṃ 
 Tāhaṃ bhumimanuppatto ṭhito saddhammamācalo 
  
                  
  
     Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samuhatā 
 Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Svāgataṃ vata me āsi buddhaseṭṭhassa santike 
 Tisso vijjā anuppattā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ānanado thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ānandattherāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Buddhavaggo paṭhamo 
 Uddānaṃ 
 Buddho paccekabuddho ca   sāriputto ca koḷito 
 Kassapo anuruddho ca puṇṇatthero upāli ca 
 Aññāsikoṇḍaññā piṇḍolo revatānandapaṇḍito 
 Chasatāni ca paññāsa gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā 
  
   Ṭhitā calā the   Paccekasambuddho se 
  
                  
                  
  
   
  
    Sīhāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nibbute lokanāthambhi siddhatthe dipaduttame 
 Vitthārite pāvacane bāhujaññamhi sāsane 
  
     Pasannacitto sumano sihāsanamakāsahaṃ 
 Sihāsanaṃ karitvāna pādapiṭhamakāsahaṃ 
  
     Sihāsane ca vassante gharaṃ tattha akāsahaṃ 
 Tena citatappasādena tusitaṃ apapajjahaṃ 
  
     Āyamena catubbisayojanaṃ āsi tāvade 
 Vimānaṃ sukataṃ mayhaṃ vitthārena catuddasa   
  
     Sataṃ   kaññāsabhassāna parivārenti maṃ sadā 
 Soṇṇaṃmayañca palalaṅka vyambhe āsi sunimmitaṃ 
  
     Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ dibbayānaṃ upaṭṭhitaṃ 
 Pāsādā sivikā ceva upapajjanti   yadicchakaṃ 
  
     Maṇimayā ca pallaṅkā aññe sāramayā bahu 
 Nibbattanti mamaṃ sabbe sihāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Soṇṇamayā rupimayā eḷikā veḷuriyāmayā 
 Pādukā abhīrūhāmi pādapiṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammavakari tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānimi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Tesattanimbhito kappe indanāmā tayo janā 
 Dvesattatimbhito kappe tayo sumana namakā  
  
     Samasattanimbhito kappe tayo varuṇanāmakā sattaratanasampannā catudipambhi issarā 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sihāsanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sīhāsanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Ekatthambhikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Siddhatthassa bhagavato mahāpuggaṇo ahu 
 Saraṇaṅgatā ca te buddhaṃ saddahanti tathāgataṃ 
  
     Sabbe saṅgamma mantetvā māḷaṃ   kubbanti satthuno 
 Ekatthambhaṃ alabhantā vicinatti buhāvane 
   Catuddasaṃ   Sata ma satta se   Nibibattanti se   Salā se the 
  
                   
  
     Tehaṃ araññe disvāna upagamma gaṇaṃ tadā 
 Añajalimpaggahetvāna paṭipucchā gaṇaṃ ahaṃ 
  
     Te me puṭṭhā viyākaṃsu sīlavanto upāsakā 
 Māḷaṃ   mayaṃ kattukāmā ekatthambho na labbhati 
  
      Ekatthambhaṃ mamaṃ detha ahaṃ dassāmi satthuno 
 Āharissāmahaṃ thambhaṃ appossukkā bhavantu vo 
  
     Te me thambhaṃ pavecchaṃsu pasannā tuṭṭhamānasā 
 Tato paṭinivattitvā agamiṃsu sakaṃ gharaṃ 
  
     Aciraṃ gate puggaṇe thambhaṃ adāsahaṃ   tadā 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena paṭhamaṃ ussapesahaṃ 
  
     Tena cittappasādena vimānaṃ upapajjahaṃ 
 Ubbiddhaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhumaṃ   samuggataṃ 
  
     Vajjamānāsu bherisu paricāremahaṃ tadā 
 Pañcapaññāsakappambhi rājā āsiṃ yasodharo 
  
     Tatthāpi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhumaṃ samuggataṃ 
 Kuṭāgāravarūpetaṃ ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ 
  
     Ekavisatikappambhi udeno nāma khattiyo 
 Tatrapi bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ satabhumaṃ samuggataṃ 
  
     Yaṃ yaṃ yonuppajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Anubhomi sukhaṃ sabbaṃ   ekatthambhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ thambhamaddiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi ekatthambhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekatthimbhiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekatthambhikattherāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
    Nandattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumattarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Vatthaṃ khomaṃ   mayā dinnaṃ sayambhussa mahesino 
  
     Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi jalajuttaranāmako    
 Iminā vatthadānena hemavaṇṇo bhavissasi 
  
   Sālaṃ the se   Ahāsahaṃ a mu ākāsahaṃ the   Satabhuma     sattabhumaṃ se the   Anubhomi sabbametaṃ     se   Vatthuttamaṃ       Jalajuttamanāyako       theragāthaṭṭhakathāya visadisaṃ 
  
                   
  
     Dve sampatti anubhotvā kusalamulehi vodito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato kaniṭṭho tvaṃ bhavissasi 
  
     Rāgaratto sukhasilo kāmesu gedhamāyuto 
 Buddhena codito santo tadā   tvaṃ pabbajissasi 
  
     Pabbajitvāna tvaṃ tattha kulamulena codito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissasanāsavo 
  
     Satakappasahassambhi   caturo celanāmakā 
 Saṭṭhikappasahassambhi upacelā catujjanā 
  
     Pañcakappasahassambhi celāva caturo janā 
 Sattaratanasampannā catudipambhi issarā 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nanado thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Nandattherāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Cullapatthakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaro nāma jino āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Gaṇamahā vupakaṭṭho so himavante vasī tadā 
  
     Ahampi himavattamhi vasāmi assame tadā 
 Acirāgataṃ vahāvīraṃ upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Pupphacchattaṃ gahetvāna upapagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Samādhiṃ samāpajjantaṃ antarāyamakāsahaṃ   
  
     Ubhohatthehi paggayha pupphachattaṃ adāsahaṃ 
 Paṭiggahesi bhagavā padumuttaro mahāmuni 
  
     Sabbe devā attamanā himavantaṃ upenti   te 
 Sādhukāraṃ pavattesuṃ   anumodissati cakkhumā 
  
   Tato se a   Sattakappasahassambhi   Ārādhanamakāsahaṃ te 
    Evaṃ sabbattha    Pavattiṃsu ma     se the 
  
                   
  
     Idaṃ vatvāna te devā upagacchuṃ naruttamaṃ 
 Ākāse dhārayantaṃ me   padumacchattamuttamaṃ   
  
     Satapattachattaṃ   paggayha   adāsi tāpaso mamaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi  suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
     Pañcavisati kappāti devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Catuntiṃsatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
     Yaṃ yaṃ yoniṃ saṃsarati devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Abbhokāse patiṭṭhantaṃ padumaṃ dhārayissati 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā leke bhavissati 
  
     Pakāsite pāvacane manussattaṃ labhissati 
 Manomayambhi kāyambhi uttamo so bhavissati 
  
     Dve bhātaro bhavissanti ubhopi patthakavhayā 
 Anubhotvā uttamatthaṃ jotayissanti sāsanaṃ 
  
     Sohaṃ aṭṭhārasamasso   pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Visesāhaṃ na vindāmi sakyaphūttassa sāsane 
  
     Dandhā mayhaṃ gati āsi paribhūto pure ahuṃ  
 Bhātā ca maṃ panāmesi gaccha dāni sakaṃ gharaṃ 
  
     Sohaṃ panāmito santo saṃghārāmassa koṭṭhake 
 Dummano tattha aṭṭhāsiṃ sāmaññasmiṃ   apekkhavā 
  
                  
  
     Bhagavā tattha   āgañachi sisaṃ mayhaṃ parāmasi 
 Bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna saṃghārāmaṃ pavesayi 
  
     Anukampāya me satthā adāsi pādapuñachaniṃ 
 Evaṃ suddhaṃ adhiṭṭhehi ekamantaṃ svadhiṭṭhitaṃ   
  
     Hatthehi tamahaṃ gayha sariṃ kokanadaṃ ahaṃ  
 Tattha cittaṃ vimucci me arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Manomayesu kāyesu sabbattha pāramiṅgato 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cullapanthako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Cullapanthakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Dhārayantassa a mu   Padumaṃ ma the   Padumachattaṃ       Gaṇaha ma 
   So aṭṭhārasavasso haṃ the aṭṭhārasañcavasso haṃ ma     se   Ahaṃ     the   Sāsanasmiṃ the   Athe satthā a mu   Ekamannamadhiṭṭhāhaṃ ma madhiṭṭhitaṃ     se 
  
                   
  
    Piḷindivacchattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nibbute lokanāthambhī sumedhe aggapuggale 
 Pasannacitto sumano thupapujamakāsahaṃ 
  
     Ye ca khiṇāsavā tattha chaḷabhiññā mahiddhikā 
 Tehaṃ tattha samānetvā saṃghabhattaṃ akāsahaṃ 
  
     Sumedhassa bhagavato upaṭṭhāko tadā ahu 
 Sumodho nāma nāmena anumodittha so tadā 
  
     Tena cittappasādena vimānaṃ upapajjahaṃ 
 Chāḷāsitisahassāni accharāyo ramiṃsu me 
  
     Mameva anuvattanti sabbakāmehi tā sadā 
 Aññe deve atibhomi   puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Pañcavisatikappambhi varuṇo nāma khattiyo 
 Susuddhabhojano   āsiṃ cakkavatti ahaṃ tadā 
  
     Na te bījaṃ pavapanti na pi niyanti naṅgalā 
 Akaṭṭhapākimaṃ sāliṃ paribhuñajanti mānusā 
  
                  
  
     Tattha rajjaṃ karitvāna devattaṃ puna gacchahaṃ 
 Tadāpi edisā mayhaṃ nibbattā bhogasampadā 
  
     Na maṃ mittā amittā vā bhiṃsanti sababapāṇino 
 Sabbesampi piyo homi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Tiṃsakappasahassambhi yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhīkānāmi gandhālepassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe eko āsiṃ   janādhīpo 
 Mahānubhāvo rājāhaṃ   cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
     Sohaṃ pañcasu silesu ṭhapetvā janataṃ bahuṃ 
 Papetvā sugatiṃyeva devatānaṃ piyo ahuṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piḷindiccho thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Piḷīndivacchattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
   Abhihomi the   Visudadha ma se the   Āsi ma se   Rājāsiṃ     ma 
  
                   
  
    Rāhulattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Sattabhummabhi pāsāde ādāsaṃ satthariṃ   ahaṃ 
  
     Khiṇāsavasahassehi parikiṇṇo mahāmuni 
 Upāgami gandhakuṭiṃ dipadindo narāsabho 
  
     Virocento   gandhakuṭiṃ devadevo narāsabho 
 Bhikkhūsaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
     Yenāyaṃ jotitā seyyā   ādāso ca susanthato 
 Tamahaṃ nittayissāmi suṇotha mama bhāsato 
  
     Soṇṇamayā rūpimayā   atho veḷuriyāmayā 
 Nibbantissanti ādāsā   ye keci manaso piyā 
  
                  
  
     Catusaṭṭhikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Sahassakkhantuṃ cakkavatti bhavissati anattarā 
  
     Ekavisatikappambhi vimalo nāma khattiyo 
 Cāturanto vijitāvi cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
     Nagaraṃ reṇuvati nāma iṭṭhakābhi sumāpitaṃ 
 Āyāmato tīṇi sataṃ caturassasamāyutaṃ   
  
     Sudassano nāma pāsādo vissakammena nimmito    
 Kuṭāgāravarūpeto sattaratanabhusito 
  
     Dasa saddā acivittaṃ   vijjādharasamākulaṃ 
 Sudassanaṃva nagaraṃ devatānaṃ bhavissati 
  
     Pabhā niggacchate tassa uggacchanteva suriye    
 Virocessati    taṃ niccaṃ samantā aṭṭhayojanaṃ 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Tusitā so cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato atrajo so bhavissati 
  
     Sace vaseyyāgāraṃ cakkavatti bhaveyya so   
 Aṭṭhānametaṃ yaṃ tādi agāre ratimajjhagā 
  
     Nikkhamitvā agāramhā pabbajissati subbato 
 Rāhulo nāma nāmena arahā so bhavissati 
  
   Ādāsiṃ sattharaṃ     sethe adāsiṃ ma   Virocantaṃ       Ādāsiṃ sattharaṃ       Sovaṇṇamayā maṇimayā se the   Ākāse ma     the se   Caturassaṃ     se   Dasasaddāvicittaṃ taṃ ma   Uggacchantova suriyo ma se    Virovissati        Bhavissati se ma 
  
                   
  
     Kikiva aṇḍaṃ rakkheyya camarī viya vāladhiṃ 
 Nipako silasampanno evaṃ rakkhiṃ   mahāmune 
  
     Tassāhaṃ dhammamaññāya vihāsiṃ sāsane rato 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rahulo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Rāhulattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Upasenattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaraṃ bhagavantaṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Pabbhārambhi nisinnaṃ taṃ   upagacchiṃ naruttamaṃ 
  
     Kaṇikāraṃ pupphitaṃ disvā vaṇṭe   chetvānahaṃ tadā 
 Alaṅkaritvā chattambhi buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
     Piṇḍapātañca pādāsiṃ   paramannaṃ subhojanaṃ 
 Buddheṇa navame tattha samaṇe aṭṭha bhojayiṃ 
  
     Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo 
  
     Tena cittappasādena sampattimanubhossati 
 Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
  
     Ekavisatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe okkāka kulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati  
  
     Sāsane dippamānambhi manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhammanimmito 
 Upasenoti nāmena hessati satthūsāvako  
  
     Carimā vattate mayhaṃ bhavā sabbe samubhatā  
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ chetvā māraṃ savāhanaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upaseno vaṅgataputto thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Upasenavaṅgantaputtattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  Tatiyabhāṇavāraṃ  
  
   Mamaṃ rakkhi     se mamarakkhi te   Nisidantaṃ ma se   Vaṇaṭā     vaṇaṭaṃ the   Piṇḍapātaṃ upanesiṃ the  ma se     potthakesu imissā gāthāya ṭhāne  yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti bhūripaññaṃ sumedhaṣaṃ kappe to satasahasse esa buddho bhavissatī  iti ayaṃ gāthā dissati   Samattapāsādikatāya aggaṭhāne ṭhapessati ti gāthaddhopi theragāthaṭṭha kathāyaṃ dissati 
  
                   
                  
  
    Raṭṭhapālattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttarassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Varanāgo mayā dinno īsādanto urūḷhavā   
  
     Setacchattopasobhito   sakappano   sahatthipo 
 Agghāpevona taṃ sabbaṃ saṃghārāmaṃ akārayiṃ 
  
     Catupaññāsa sahasasāni pāsāde kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Mahābhattaṃ   karitvāna niyyādesiṃ mahesino 
  
     Anumodi mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Sabbe jane bhāsayanto desesi amataṃ padaṃ 
  
     Taṃ me buddho viyākāsi jalajuttaranāmako    
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gātha abhāsatha 
  
     Catupaññasa sahassāni pāsāde kārayī ayaṃ 
 Kathayissāmi vipākaṃ suṇetha mama bhāsato 
  
     Aṭṭhārasa sahassāni kuṭāgārā bhavissare 
 Vyamahuttamambhī nibbattā sabbasoṇṇamayā ca te 
  
     Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karisasati 
 Aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Aḍḍhe kule mahābhoge nibbattissati tāmade 
  
     So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Raṭṭhapāloti nāmena hessati satthūsāvako 
  
     Padhānapahitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
     Uṭṭhāya abhinikkhamma jahitā   bheghasampadā 
 Kheḷapiṇḍeva bhogambhi pemaṃ mayhaṃ na vijjati 
  
                  
  
     Virāyaṃ me dhūradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā raṭṭhapālo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Raṭṭhapālattherassa apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
   Urūḷabhavo       Chattopasevito     se chatto sopadhiko ma the 
   Sādabbino ma sidabbano the   Mahoghañca ma se a mahaṅghañca the   Jalajuttamanāyako       Jahitvā ma te se 
  
                   
  
    Sopākattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Pabbhāraṃ sevayantassa   vipine   pabbatuttame 
 Siddhattho nāma bhagavā āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
     Buddhaṃ upāgataṃ disvā lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Sattharaṃ santharitvāna   pupphasanamādāsahaṃ 
  
     Pupphāsane nisīditvā siddhattho lokanāyako 
 Mamañca gatimaññāya aniccatamudāhi 
  
      Aniccā vana saṅkhārā uppādavayadhammino 
 Upapajjitvā nirujjhanti tesaṃ vupasamo sukho  
  
     Idaṃ vatvāna sababaññu lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Nahaṃ abbhūggami dhīro haṃsarājāva ambare 
  
     Sakaṃ diṭṭhaṃ jahitvāna bhāvayāniccasaññahaṃ 
 Ekāhaṃ bhāvayitvāna tattha kālakato ahaṃ 
  
     Dve sampatti anubhotvā sukkamūlena codito 
 Pacchībhave sampatte sapākayonupāgamiṃ   
  
     Agārā abhinikkhamma pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Āraddhaviriyo pahitatto sīlesu susamāhito 
 Tosetvānamahānāgaṃ alatthaṃ upasampadaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Vatunavute ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pupphadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ saññaṃ bhāvayiṃ tadā 
 Taṃ saññaṃ bhāvayantassa patto me āsavakkhayo 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sopāko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sopākattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
    Sumaṅgalattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Āhutiṃ yiṭṭhukāmohaṃ paṭiyādetvāna bhojanaṃ 
 Brāhmaṇe patimānento visāle māḷake ṭhito 
  
     Athaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ 
 Sabbalokavinetāraṃ sayambhuṃ aggapuggalaṃ 
  
     Bhagavantaṃ jutimantaṃ sāvakehi purakkhataṃ 
 Ādiccamiva rocantaṃ rathiyaṃ paṭipannakaṃ   
  
   Sodhayantassa     sobhayattassa se   Papare     pavane se pavare the   Paññapetvāna Se te   Sopākaṃ the   Pavisantakaṃ      theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ pana visadisaṃ apadānaṃ paññāyati tampana dvādasamavagge sumaṅgalāpadānne sameti 
  
                   
  
     Añajalimpaggahetvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Manasā ca nimantesiṃ āgacchatu mahāmuniti 
  
     Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro 
 Khiṇāsavasahassehi mama dvāraṃ upāgami 
  
      Namo te purisājañña namo te purisuttama 
 Pāsādaṃ abhirūhitvā sihāsane nisida tvaṃ  
  
     Danto dantaparivāro tiṇṇo tārayataṃ varo 
 Pāsādaṃ abhirūhitvā nisīdi pavarāsane 
  
     Yaṃ me atthi sake gehe āmisaṃ paccupaṭṭhitaṃ 
 Tāhaṃ buddhassa pādāsiṃ pasanno sehi pāṇihi 
  
     Pasannacitto sumano vedajāto katañajalī 
 Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ namassāmi aho buddhassuḷāratā 
  
                  
  
     Aṭṭhannaṃ payirūpāsataṃ   bhuñjaṃ   khiṇāsavā bahu 
 Tuyheveso ānubhāvo saraṇaṃ taṃ upemahaṃ 
  
     Piyadassī ca bhagavā lokajeṭṭho narāsabho 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Yo so saṃghaṃ abhojesi ujubhūtaṃ samāhitaṃ 
 Tathāgatañca sambuddhaṃ suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
     Sattavisatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Sakakammābhiraddho so devaloke ramissati 
  
     Dasañcaṭṭhakkhattuṃ so cakkatti bhavissati 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ pañcasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati  
  
     Araññaṃ vanamogayha kātanaṃ vyagghasevitaṃ 
 Padhānaṃ padahitvāna kiso jhāpitā mayā 
  
     Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhījānāmi bhattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumaṅgalo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sumaṅgalattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
  Uddānaṃ 
 Sīhāsani ekathambhi nando cullapanthako 
 Piḷindo   rāhulo ceva vaṅganto raṭṭhapālako 
 Sopāko maṅgalo ceva daseva dutiye vagge 
 Satañca aṭṭhatiṃsā ca gāthā ettha pakāsitā 
   Sihāsanadāyakavaggo dutiyo   
  
   Payirupāsaṃ ma    Sabbattha    Piḷinda ma piḷindi se 
  
                   
                  
  
    Subhūtittherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Himavantassa avidūre nisabho nāma pabbato 
 Assamo sukato mayhaṃ paṇṇasālā sumāpitā 
  
     Kosiyo nāma nāmena jaṭilo uggatāpano 
 Ekākiyo adutiyo vasāmi nisabhe tadā 
  
     Phalaṃ mulañca paṇṇañca na bhūñajami ahaṃ tadā 
 Pavattapaṇḍupattāni   upajivāmi tāvade 
  
     Nāhaṃ kopemi ājīvaṃcajamānopi jīvitaṃ 
 Ārādhemi sakaṃ cittaṃ vivajjemi anesataṃ 
  
     Rugupasaṃhitaṃ cittaṃ yadā upapajjane mama 
 Sayaṃva paccavekkhāmi ekaggo taṃ dammehaṃ 
  
      Rajjasi rajaniye ca dosaniye ca dussasi  
 Muyhase mohaniye ca nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ 
  
     Visuddhānaṃ ayaṃ vāso nimmalānaṃ tapassinaṃ 
 Mā kho visuddhaṃ dusesi nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ 
  
     Agāriko bhavitvāna sadā yuttaṃ   labhissasi 
 Ubhopi mā virādhesi nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ 
  
     Chavālātaṃ yathā kaṭṭhaṃ na kvaci kiccakārakaṃ    
 Neva gāme araññe vā na hi taṃ kaṭṭhasammataṃ 
  
     Chavālātupamo tvaṃsi na gihi nāpi saññato    
 Ubhato muttako ajja nikkhamassu vanā tuvaṃ 
  
     Siyā nu kho tava   etaṃ ko papajānāti te   idaṃ 
 Saddhādhūraṃ jahasi   te  kosajjabahulāya ca 
  
     Jigucchissanti taṃ viññu asuciṃ nāgariko yathā 
 Ākaḍḍhitvāna isayo codayissanti taṃ sadā 
  
     Taṃ viññu pavadissanti samatikkantasāsanaṃ 
 Saṃvāsaṃ alabhanto hi kathaṃ jivissasi   tuvaṃ 
  
   Pavattaṃca supātābhaṃ ma se pattāhaṃ       Dussase the ma   Yadā puttaṃ ma the   Kāraṇaṃ ma the   Gihinā nāpi paññatto       Tuvaṃ ma   Ko pajānihite     se   Pāhisi     vahasi ma pahāsi the piṅgaduraṃpahisi se  me   Jivāhisi se ma jivihisi     the 
  
                   
                  
  
     Tidhā pabhinnamātaṅgaṃ kuñajaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ 
 Khali nāgo upagantvā yuthā niharate gajaṃ 
  
     Yuthā vinissaṭo santo sukhaṃ sātaṃ na vindati 
 Dukkhito vimano   hoti pajjhāyanto   pavadheti   
  
     Tatheva jaṭilā tampi niharissanti dummatiṃ  
 Tehi tvaṃ nissaṭo santo sukhaṃ sātaṃ na lacchasi 
  
     Divā yā yadi vā rattiṃ sokasallasamappito 
 Ḍayhasi pariḷāhena gajo yuthāva nissaṭo   
  
     Jātarūpaṃ yathā kūṭaṃ neva jhāpeti   katthaci 
 Tathā silavibhino tvaṃ na jhāpessasi   katthaci 
  
     Agāraṃ vasamānopi kathaṃ jiviśisi tuvaṃ 
 Mattikaṃ pettikaṃ cāpi natthi te nibhitaṃ   dhanaṃ 
  
     Sayaṃ   kammaṃ karitvāna gatte sedaṃ pamocayaṃ 
 Evaṃ jivihisi gehe sādhu te taṃ    na ruccati  
  
     Evāhaṃ tattha vāremi    saṅkilesagataṃ manaṃ 
 Nānādhammamakathaṃ katvā pāpā cittā nivārayiṃ 
  
     Evaṃ me viharantassa appamādavihārino 
 Tiṃsa vassasahassāni vipine me    atikkamuṃ 
  
     Appamādarataṃ disvā uttamatthagavesakaṃ 
 Padumuttarasambuddho āgacchi mama santikaṃ 
  
     Timbarūsakavaṇṇabho    appameyyo anupamo 
 Rūpenasadiso buddho ākāse caṅkamī tadā 
  
     Suphūllo sālarājāva vijjūvabbhaghanantare   
 Ñāṇenāsadiso buddho ākāse caṅkami tadā 
  
     Sīharājāvasambhito gajarājāva dappito 
 Lasito    vyaggharājāva ākāse caṅkami tadā 
  
     Siṃginikkhasuvaṇṇābho khadiraṅgārasannibho 
 Maṇi yathā jotiraso ākāse caṅkami tadā 
  
                  
  
     Visuddhakelāsanibho puṇṇamāyeva    candimā 
 Majjhantikeva    suriyo ākāse caṅkami tadā 
  
   Dummano the   Ujjhā       Padhācati       Dumamati     se   Yuthā vinissaṭo a mu   Jhāyati yāyati       Nevayāsi     jhāyissasi   Nicitaṃ the   Sakaṃ     se    Kiṃ the    Dhāremi se    Pavaneva me     se pavaneva the    Durāsado the    Māseva      se    Kova      se 
  
                   
  
     Disvā nabhe   caṅkamantaṃ evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
  Devo nu kho ayaṃ satto udāhu manujo ayaṃ  
  
     Na me suto vā diṭṭho vā mabhiyā ediso naro 
 Api mantapadaṃ atthi ayaṃ satthā bhavissati   
  
     Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ 
 Nānāpuppañca gandhañca santipātetvahaṃ   tadā 
  
     Pupphāsanaṃ paññapetvā sādhucittaṃ manoramaṃ 
 Narasārathinaṃ aggaṃ idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  
      Idaṃ me āsanaṃ vīra paññattaṃ tavanucchaviṃ  
 Hāsayanto mamaṃ cittaṃ nisida kusumāsane  
  
     Nisīdi tattha bhagavā asambhitova kesarī 
 Sattarattindivaṃ buddho pavare kusumāsane 
  
     Namassamāno aṭṭhāsiṃ sattarattindivaṃ ahaṃ 
 Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimbhā satthā loke anuttaro 
  
     Mama kammaṃ pakittento idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ 
  Bhāvehi buddhānussatiṃ bhāvanānamanuttaraṃ 
  
     Imaṃ satiṃ bhāvayitvā purayissasi mānasaṃ    
 Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissasi 
  
     Asitikkhantuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ cakkavatti rājā raṭṭhe bhavissasi 
  
     Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
 Anubhossasi taṃ sabbaṃ buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ 
  
     Bhavābhave saṃsaranto mahābhogaṃ labhīssasi 
 Bhoge te ūnatā natthi buddhanussatiyā phalaṃ 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Asitikoṭiṃ chaḍḍhetvā dāse   kammakare bahu 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissasi 
  
     Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Subhūti nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako 
  
   Disvāna taṃ ma disvāna taṃ nabhe the   Santipātesa haṃ maṃ   Nucchakaṃ se   Purayassu sumātasaṃ the   Pesa Se 
  
                   
                  
  
     Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā dakkhiṇeyyaguṇambhi taṃ    
 Tathāraṇavihāre ca   dvisu agge ṭhapessati   
  
     Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho jalajuttaranāmako    
 Nabhaṃ abbhūggami dhīro haṃsarājāva ambare 
  
     Sāsito lokanātheṇa namassitvā tathāgataṃ 
 Sadā bhāvemi   mudito buddhānussatimuttamaṃ 
  
     Tena kammena sukatena cetanā paṇidhi hi ca 
 Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ 
  
     Asitikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
  
     Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇaṇāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
 Anubhomi susampattiṃ buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ 
  
     Bhāvābhave saṃsaranno mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
 Bhoge me ūnatā natthi buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ 
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhīkānāmi buddhānussatiyā phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā subhūtithero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Subhūtittherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    Upavānatthepadānaṃ 
  
     Padumuttaro nāma jino sabbadhammāna pāragu 
 Jalitvā aggikkhandhova sambuddho parinibbuto 
  
     Mahājanā samāgamma pujayitvā tathāgataṃ 
 Citaṃ   katvāna sukataṃ sarīraṃ abhīropayuṃ 
  
                  
  
     Sarīrakiccaṃ katvāna dhātuṃ   tattha samānayuṃ 
 Sadevamānusā sabbe buddhathupaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
     Paṭhamā kañcanamayā dutiyāsi maṇimayā 
 Tatiyā rūpiyamayā catutthā   phaḷikāmayā 
  
     Tathā pañcamiyā nemi   lohitaṅkamayā ahu 
 Chaṭṭhā masāragallassa sabbaratanamayupari 
  
   Etadagge ṭhapessati the ṇeyyaguṇehi ma   Vihārena ma araṇavihāre dakkhiṇeyye the   Visu ṭhānasu gotamo the   Jalajuttamanāyako     se   Bhāvesiṃ   Citakaṃ a mu   Dhātu       Catutthi ma se the 
   Pañca mikācehi ma     se tattha pañcamikā ceti the 
  
                   
  
     Jaṅghā maṇimayā āsi vedikā ratanāmayā 
 Sababasovaṇṇayo thupo uddhaṃ yojanamuggato 
  
     Devā tattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Mayampi thupaṃ kassāma lokanāthassa tādino 
  
     Dhātu āveṇikā natthi sarīraṃ ekapiṇḍitaṃ 
 Imambhi buddhathupambhi kassāma kañcukaṃ mayā  
  
     Devā sattaratanehi   aññaṃ vaḍḍhesu yojanaṃ 
 Thupo dviyojanubbedho timiraṃ vyapahanti so 
  
     Nāgā tattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Manussā ceva devā ca buddhathupaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
     Mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā 
 Mayampi thupaṃ kassāma lokanāthassa tādino  
  
     Indanilaṃ mahānīlaṃ atho jotirasaṃ maṇiṃ 
 Ekato sannipatetvā buddhathupaṃ achādayuṃ 
  
     Sabbaṃ maṇimayaṃ āsi tāvatā buddhacetiyaṃ 
 Tiṃsayojanamu  bbadhaṃ   ālokakaraṇaṃ tadā 
  
     Garuḷā   ca samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Manusā devā nāgā ca buddhāthupaṃ akaṃsu te 
  
     Mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā 
 Mayampi thupaṃ kassā ma lokanāthassa tādino 
  
     Sabbamaṇimayaṃ thupe   akaruttarakañcukaṃ    
 Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ 
  
     Catuyojanamubbiddho   buddhathupo virocati 
 Obhāseti disā sabbā sataraṃsiva uggato  
  
                  
  
     Kumbhaṇḍā ca samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Manussā ceva devā ca nāgā ca garuḷā   tathā 
  
     Paccekaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa akaṃsu thupamuttamaṃ 
 Mā no pattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā 
  
     Mayampi thupaṃ kassāma lokanāthassa tādino 
 Ratanehi chādayissāma āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ 
  
     Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ 
 Pañcayojanamubbiddho obhāsate tadā 
  
  Garūḷā ti ādayo catasso gāthāyo se     potthakesu na vijjanti   Sattahi rattehi ma se   Mubbiddhaṃ a mu   Kumbhaṇḍā     the   Sabbaṃ manimayaṃ thupaṃ ma the   Akaruṃ te ca kañcukaṃ ma se the    Mubbedho the   Nāgā kumbhaṇḍakā the 
  
                   
  
     Yakkhā nattha samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Manussā devanāgā ca garuḷā kumbhaaṇḍakā 
  
     Paccekaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa akaṃsu thupamuttamaṃ 
 Mā no pamattā assumhā appamattā sadevakā 
  
     Mayampi thupaṃ kassāma lokanāthassa tādino 
 Eḷikāhi   chādayissāma āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ 
  
     Yojanaṃ tepi vaḍḍhesuṃ āyataṃ buddhacetiyaṃ 
 Cha tyājanāni ubbiddho thūpo obhāsate tadā 
  
     Gandhabbā ca samāgantvā ekato mantayuṃ tadā 
  Manujā devatā nāgā kumbhaṇḍā guruḷā tathā 
  
     Sabbekaṃsu   buddhathupaṃ mayamettha akārakā 
 Mayampi thupaṃ kassāma lokanāthassa tādino 
  
     Vediyo satta katvāna chattamāropayiṃsu te  
 Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ   thupaṃ gandhabbaṃ kārayuṃ tadā  
  
     Sattayojanamubbiddho thupo obhāsete tadā 
 Rattindivā na cāyanti āloko hoti   sabbadā 
  
     Abhībhonti na tassāhā candasurā satārakā 
 Samantā yojanasate padipopi na pajjali 
  
     Tena kālena ye keci thupaṃ pujenti mānusā 
 Na te thūpamāruhanti ambare ukkhipanti te 
  
     Devehi ṭhapito yakkho abhīsammata nāmako 
 Dhajaṃ vā pupphadāmaṃ vā abhiropeti uttari 
  
     Na te passanti taṃ yakkhaṃ dāmaṃ passanti gacchato 
 Evaṃ passitvā gacchantā   sabbe gacchanti suggatiṃ 
  
     Visaddhā   ye pāvavane pasannā ye ca sāsane 
 Pāṭibhīraṃ daṭṭhaṭukāmā thūpaṃ pujenti mānusā 
  
     Nagare haṃsavatiyā ahosiṃ bhatako   tadā 
 Āmoditaṃ janaṃ disvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
  
      Uḷāro bhagavā heso    yassa dhātughatadisā 
 Imā ca janatā tuṭṭhākāraṃ kubbantatappakaṃ    
  
     Ahmapi kāraṃ kassāmi lokanāthassa tādino 
 Tassa dhammesu dāyādo bhavissāmi anāgate 
  
   Phalikaṃ a mu   Kumbhaṇḍāguyahakā tathā     garuḷā kumbhāṇḍakā a mu   Kathā ma       Yāva jaṅghā akaṃsu te     se dhajaṃ chattamakaṃsu te the   Sabbāsocaṇṇayaṃ       Ālokā honti ma   Gacchanti ma   Viruddhā ma the   Varako ma vadako     se    Neso ma     se the    Kubbaṃ na tappare ma the kubbanti tappare      kumbhaṇḍādinaṃ paṭipāṭiyā visadisatā ekaccesu dissati     se the potthakesu chayojanubbedhatā na vuttā garuḷā ca vajjitā 
  
                   
                  
  
     Sudhotaṃ rajakenāhaṃ uttareyyapaṭaṃ mama 
 Veḷagge ālagetvāna dhajaṃ ukkhīpimbare 
  
     Abhīyammatako gayha ambarehāsi me dhajaṃ 
 Vātaritaṃ dhajaṃ disvā vipākaṃ pucchahaṃ dhaje 
  
     Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā samaṇaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ 
 Taṃ bhikkhūṃ abhivādetvā vipākaṃ pucchahaṃ dhaje 
  
     So me kathesi ānandapitisañajanataṃ mama 
  Tassa dhajassa vipākaṃ anubheṣsasi sabbadā 
  
     Hatthi assā rathā patti senā ca caturaṅgini 
 Parivāressanti   taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Saṭṭhi turiyasahassāni bheriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Parivāressanti taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Chaḷāsitisahassāni nāriyo samalaṅkatā 
 Vicittavatthābhaṇā āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā 
  
     Aḷārapamhā hasulā susaṇhā   tanumajjhimā 
 Parivāressanti taṃ niccaṃ dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
     Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissasi 
 Asitikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjaṃ karissasi 
  
     Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca cakkavatti bhavissasi 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhīyaṃ 
  
     Kappasatasahassambhī okakāka kulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
     Delokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Puññakammena saṃyutto brahmabandhu bhavissasi 
  
     Asitikoṭiṃ chaḍḍhetvā dāse kammakare bahu 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissasi 
  
     Ārādhayitvā sambuddhaṃ gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ 
 Upavānoti nāmena hessasi satthu sāvako ti 
  
     Satasahasse kataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
 Sumuttasaravegova kilese jhāpayī   mama 
  
     Cakkavattissa santassa catudipissarassa me 
 Tiyojanāni sāmantā   ussīyanti dhajā sadā 
  
                  
  
     Satasahasse ito kappe yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhajadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upavāno thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Upavānattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
   Parivārenti       Sutthanā the susaññā bahūsu   Kilesā jhāpitā the   Tīṇi yojana sāmattā se the 
  
                   
  
    Saraṇagamaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nagare candavatiyā   mātupaṭṭhāyako ahuṃ 
 Andhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ te posemi ahaṃ tadā 
  
     Rahogato nisīditvā evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā 
 Posento mātāpitare pabbajjaṃ na labhāmahaṃ 
  
     Tamandhakārapihitā   tividhaggihi ḍayhare 
 Etādise bhatya   jāte natthi koci vināyako 
  
     Buddho loke samuppanno dippati jinasāsanaṃ 
 Sakkā uddharituṃ   attā puññakammeta   jantunā 
  
     Uggayha tīṇi saraṇe pharipuṇṇaṇī gopayiṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena paṭimokkhāmi   duggati 
  
     Nisabho nāma samaṇo buddhassa aggasāvako 
 Tamahaṃ upagantvāna saraṇāgamanaṃ gahiṃ 
  
     Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāmade 
 Tāvatā saraṇagamanaṃ paripuṇṇaṃ agopayiṃ 
  
     Carime vattamānambhi saraṇaṃ taṃ anussariṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena tāvatiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
     Devalokagato santo puññakammasamābhito 
 Yaṃ desaṃ upagacchāmi   aṭṭha hetu labhāmahaṃ 
  
     Disāsu pujito homi tikkhaphañño bhanāmahaṃ 
 Sabbe devānuvattanti amitabhegaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Suvaṇṇaṇṇo sabbattha paṭikanto bhavāmahaṃ 
 Mittānaṃ acalo homi yaso accugagato   mama 
  
     Asitikkhattuṃ devindo devarajjamakārayiṃ 
 Dibbaṃ sukhaṃ anubhaviṃ accharāhi purakkhato 
  
     Pañcasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti abhosahaṃ 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ 
  
     Pacchimabhave sampatte puññakammasamāhito 
 Pure sāvatthiyaṃ jāto mahāsalo su aḍḍhake 
  
     Nagarā nikkhamitvāna dārakehi purakkhato 
 Hāsakhiḍḍhāsamaṃgihaṃ   saṅghārāmaṃ upāgami 
  
     Tatthaddasāsiṃ samaṇaṃ vippamuttaṃ nirūpadhiṃ 
 So me dhammadesesi saraṇañaca adāsi me 
  
   Bandhumatiyā se a   Mahandhakārapihitā   Bhave ma se   Uttarituṃ se   Puññakāmena se   Pari       Upapajjāmi ma    se   Abbhuggato ma   Sahasā khiḍḍa se      tisaraṇagamaniyattherāpadāna ma 
  
                   
  
     Sohaṃ sutvāna saraṇaṃ me anussariṃ 
 Ekāsane nisīditvā arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Jātiyā sattavassena arahattaṃ apāpuṇiṃ 
 Upasampādesi   sambuddho guṇamaññā cakkhumā 
  
     Aparimeyye ito kappe saraṇāni agacchihaṃ 
 Tato me sukataṃ kammaṃ phalaṃ dassesi me idha 
  
     Sugopitaṃ me saraṇaṃ mānasaṃ suppaṇihitaṃtha 
 Anuśotvā yasaṃ sabbaṃ patetāmbhi acalaṃ padaṃ 
  
     Yesaṃ sotāvadhānatthi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
 Ahaṃ   vo kathayissāmi sāmaṃ diṭṭhaṃ padaṃ   mama 
  
      Buddho loke samuppanno vattate jinasāsanaṃ 
 Amatā vāditā bherī sokasallavinodanā 
  
     Yathā sakena thāmena puññakkhette anuttare 
 Adhikāraṃ kareyyātha phassayissatha   nibbutiṃ 
  
     Paggayha tīṇi saraṇe pañca sīlāni gopiya  
 Buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā dukkhassantaṃ karissatha 
  
                  
  
     Mamopamaṃ karitvāna   sīlāni parigopiya 
 Aciraṃ arahattaṃ vo sabbepi pāpuṇissatha  
  
     Tevijjo iddhipattombi cetopariyakovido 
 Sāvako te mahāvīra caraṇe   vandati satthuno 
  
     Aparimeyye ito kappe saraṇaṃ buddhassa gacchataṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi saraṇāgamane phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nisaraṇagamaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Tisaraṇagamaniyattherassāpadānaṃ   tatiyaṃ   
  
    Pañcasīlasamādāniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nagare candavatiyā bhatako āsahaṃ tadā 
 Parakammāyane yutto pabbajjaṃ labhāmahaṃ 
  
     Tamandhakārapihitā   tividhagagihi    ḍayahare 
 Kena nu kho upāyena visaṃyutto bhave ahaṃ 
  
     Deyyadhammo ca me natthi varāko bhatako    ahaṃ 
 Yannunāhaṃ pañcasīlaṃ rakkheyyaṃ paripurayaṃ 
  
   Upasampādayī ma   Atthaṃ se   Diṭṭhamidaṃ     diṭṭhapadaṃ se   Passayissatha  sabbattha    Gopaya se       Sammā dhammaṃ bhāvetvā ma 
   Saraṇo ma ṣe saraṇo       Saraṇegamaniya ma   Mahandhakāra pihitā se    Tividhaggi pi        Bhatako dukkhito ma 
  
                   
  
     Anomadassi   munino nisabho nāma sāvako 
 Tamahaṃ upasaṅkamma pañcasikkhāpadaggahiṃ 
  
     Vassasatasahassāni āyu vijjati tāvade 
 Tāvatā pañca sīlāni paripuṇṇāni gopayiṃ 
  
     Maccukālambhi   sampatte devā assāsayanti maṃ 
 Ratho sahassassayutto mārisāyaṃ   upaṭṭhito 
  
     Vattante   carime citte mama sīlaṃ anussariṃ 
 Tena kammena sukatena tātiṃsaṃ agacchahaṃ 
  
                  
  
     Tiṃsakkhattuñca devindo devarajjaṃ akārayiṃ 
 Dibbaṃ sukhaṃ anubhaviṃ accharābhi purakkhato 
  
     Pañcasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti ahosahaṃ 
 Papadesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
     Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Pure vesāliyaṃ jāto mahāsāle suaḍḍhake 
  
     Vassupanāyike kāle dippante jinasāsane 
 Mātā ca me pitā ceva pañcasikkhāpadaggahuṃ 
  
     Saha sutenahaṃ sīghaṃ mama sīlaṃ anussariṃ 
 Ekāsane nisīditvā arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
     Jātiyā pañcavassehaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
 Upasampādayī buddho guṇamaññāya cakkhumā 
  
     Paripuṇṇāni gopetvā pañca sikkhāpadānahaṃ 
 Aparimeyye ito kappe vitipātaṃ na gacchahaṃ 
  
     Svāhaṃ yasamanubhaviṃ tesaṃ silānavāhasā 
 Kappakoṭimpi kittento kitteyya ekadesakaṃ 
  
     Pañca sīlāni gopetvā tayo hetu labhāmahaṃ 
 Dīghāyuto mahābhogo tikkhapañño bhavāmahaṃ 
  
     Pakittento   va sabbesaṃ adhimattañca porisaṃ 
 Bhavābhave saṃsaritvā ete ṭhane labhāmahaṃ 
  
     Aparimayya sīlesu vattanto jinasāvako    
 Bhavesu yadi rajjeyya   vipāko kidiso bhave 
  
   Dasasissa ma     se   Kāle ca ma   Māriyassa ma   Marisassa ma   Sampatte       Saṃkittento ma       Vattantā jinasāvakā ma   Rajjayyeṃ ma 
  
                   
  
     Suciṇṇaṃ me pañcasīlaṃ bhatakena vipassinā 
 Tena sīlenahaṃ ajja mocayiṃ   sabbabandhanaṃ 
  
     Aparimeyye ito kappe pañca silāni gopayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pañcasīlānidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcasīlasamādāniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcasīlasamādāniyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Annasaṃsāvakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe 
 Tañcanagghiyasaṅkāsaṃ dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ 
  
     Siddhatthaṃ lokapajjotaṃ appameyyaṃ anopamaṃ 
 Alatthaṃ paramaṃ pitiṃ disvā dantaṃ jutindharaṃ 
  
     Sambuddhaṃ abhimattetvā   bhojayiṃ taṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Mahākāruṇiko   nātho   anumodi mamaṃ tadā 
  
     Tasmiṃ mahākāruṇike parassāsakārake 
 Buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ 
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā annasaṃsāvako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Annasaṃsāvakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    Dhupadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Siddhatthassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Kuṭidhupaṃ   mayā dinnaṃ vippasannena cetasā 
  
     Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sabbesampi piyo homi dhupadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Poṭhayiṃ       Atināmetvā abināmetvā ma se   Muni kāruṇiko       Loke ma   Kuṭidhupanaṃ     se 
  
                   
  
     Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ dhupaṃ adadiṃ tadā    
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi dhupadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhupadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dhupādāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Pulinapujakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Vipassissa bhagavato bodhiyā pādaputtame 
 Purāṇapulinaṃ chaḍḍetvā suddhaṃ pulinamākiriṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito kappeyaṃ pulinamadāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi pulinadānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Tipaññāse   ito kappe rājā āsiṃ janādhibhu 
 Mahāpulina nāmena   cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinapujako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pulinapujakattherassāpadānaṃ satatamaṃ   
  
    Uttariyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Candabhāgānaditire suṃsumāro ahaṃ tadā 
 Sagocarappasutohaṃ   tadititthaṃ agañachahaṃ 
  
     Siddhattho tambhi samaye sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Nadiṃ taritukāmo so nadititthaṃ upāgami 
  
     Upāgate ca   sambuddhe ahampi tatthupāgamiṃ 
 Upagantvāna sambabuddhaṃ imaṃ vācaṃ udirayiṃ 
  
     Abhirūha mahāvīra tāressāmi ahaṃ tuvaṃ 
 Pettikaṃ visayaṃ mayhaṃ anukampa mahāmune 
  
     Mama uggajjanaṃ sutvā abhirūhi mahāmuni 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena tāresiṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
     Nadiyā pārime tīre siddhattho lokanayako 
 Assāsesi mamaṃ tattha amataṃ pāpuṇissasi 
  
   Yaṃ dhupanamadāsahaṃ ma se   Tiṃsatime ma   Mahāpulino     se   Sabhojana se       Upāgatambhi 
  
                   
  
     Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna devalokaṃ agacachahaṃ 
 Dibbaṃ sukhaṃ anubhaviṃ accharābhi purakkhato 
  
     Sattakkhattuñca devindo devarajjaṃ akasahaṃ 
 Tīṇikkhattuṃ cakkavatti mabhiyā issaro ahuṃ 
  
                  
  
     Vivekamanuyuttohaṃ nipako ca susaṃvuto 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
     Catunavute ito kappe tāresiṃ yaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi tāraṇāya   idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uttariyayo   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Uttariyattherassāpadānaṃ   aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    Ekañajalikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ gacchantaṃ antarāpaṇe 
 Vipassiṃ satthavāhaggaṃ naraviraṃ vinayakaṃ 
  
     Adantadamakaṃ   tādiṃ mahāvādiṃ mahāmatiṃ  
 Disvā pasanno sumano ekañcalaṃmakāsahaṃ 
  
     Ekanavute ito kappe yamañajaliṃ kariṃ   tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
     Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekañjaliko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Ekañajalikattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
    Khomadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
     Nagare bandhumatiyā ahosiṃ vāṇijo tadā 
 Teneva dāraṃ posemi ropemi bījasampadaṃ 
  
     Rathiyaṃ paṭipannassa vipassissa mahesino 
 Ekaṃ khomaṃ mayā dinnaṃ kusalatthāya satthuno 
  
   Taraṇāya ma     se   Uttiro ma uttiyo       Uttira ma uttiya       Damanaṃ ma     daminaṃ se   Mahāmuniṃ       Añajalimakariṃ ma 
  
                   
                  
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattavise ito kappe eko sindhavasandano 
 Sattaratanasampanenā catudipambhi issaro 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā khomadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Khomadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Subhūti upavāno ca saraṇo silagāhako 
 Antasaṃsāvako dhupo pulino uttariyena   ca 
 Añajali khomadāyi ca daseva tatiye gaṇe 
 Pañcāsiti sataṃ vuttā gāthāyo sabbapiṇḍitā 
   Subhūtivaggo tatiyo   
  
 Catutthaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ 
  
    Kuṇḍadhānattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Patatāhaṃ paṭisallinaṃ sayambhuṃ aggapuggalaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upaṭṭhabhiṃ 
  
      Vuṭṭhitaṃ kālamaññāya padumuttaraṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Mahantiṃ   kadalikaṇṇiṃ gahetvā upagañachahaṃ 
  
      Paṭiggahetvā   bhagavā taṃ phalaṃ   lokanāyako 
 Mama cittaṃ pasādento paribhuñaji mahāmuni 
  
      Paribhuñajitvāna sambuddho satthavāho anuttaro 
 Sakāsane   nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
                  
  
       Ye vasanti sametāro   yakkhā imambhi pabbate 
 Araññe bhūtabhavyāti suṇantu vacanaṃ mama 
  
      Yo so budadhaṃ upaṭṭhāsi   migarājā ca kesarī   
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
   Uttiyena       Mahantaṃ the       Paṭiggahesi ma se   Sabbaññu ma se   Ekāsane se   Ye ca santi samitāro ma se   Yo maṃ upaṭṭhahi poso the   Migarājaṃva kesariṃ ma 
  
                   
  
      Soyamekādasakkhattuṃ   devarājā bhavissati 
 Catuttiṃsakkhattuñca   cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Akkoyitvāna samaṇe silavante anāsave 
 Pāpakammavipākena nāmadheyyaṃ labhissati 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyādo oraso dhama nimmito 
 Kuṇḍadhānoti nāmena sāvako so bhavissati 
  
      Pavivekamanuyutto jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ 
 Tosayitvāna satthāraṃ viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Sāvakaggehi   parivuto bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā sālākaṃ gāhayī jino 
  
      Ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā vanditvā lokanāyakaṃ 
 Vadataṃ varassa purato paṭhamaṃ agagahesahaṃ 
  
      Tena kammena bhagavā asasahassipakampako 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Viriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṇḍadhāno thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kuṇḍadhānattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Sāgatattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sobhito nāma nāmena ahosiṃ buhmaṇe tadā 
 Purakkhato sasissehi ārāmaṃ agamāsahaṃ 
  
      Bhagavā tambhi samaye bhikkhusaṅghapurakkhato 
 Ārāmadvārā tikkhamma aṭṭhāsi purisuttamo 
  
      Tamaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ dantaṃ dantaparakkhataṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
   Ekādasañcakkhattuṃ so ma   Catuvisatikkhattuñca the catutiṃsati ma se   Bhavissati ma   Sāvakehi se ma 
  
                   
  
       Ye keci pādapā sabbe mabhiyā te virūhare 
 Buddhimanto tathā sattā rūhanti jinasāsate 
  
      Satthavāhosi sappañño mahesī   bahuke jane 
 Vipathā uddharitvāna pathaṃ ācikkhase tuvaṃ 
  
      Danto antaparikiṇṇo jhāyī jhānaratehi ca 
 Ātāpi pahitattehi upasantehi tādihi 
  
      Alaṅkato parisāhi   puññāṇehi   sobhasi 
 Pabhā niddhāvate tuyhaṃ suriyodayane   yathā 
  
      Pasannacittaṃ disvāna mahesī padumuttaro 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satho imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Yo so bhāsaṃ janetvāna mamaṃ kittesi brāhmaṇo 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ devaloke ramissati 
  
      Tusitā hi cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati 
  
      Tena kammena sukatena   arahattaṃ   labhissati 
 Sāgato nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako 
  
      Pabbajitvāna kāyena pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ 
 Vaciduccaritaṃ hitvā ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ 
  
                  
  
      Evaṃ viharamānohaṃ tejodhātusu kovido 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāmavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sāgato thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sāgatattherassāpadānaṃ datiyaṃ   
  
    Mahākaccānattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaranāthassa padumaṃ nāma cetiyaṃ 
 Silasanaṃ   kārayitvā suvaṇṇenābhilepayiṃ 
  
      Ratanāmayachattañca paggayha vāḷavijaniṃ 
 Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ lokabandhussa tādino 
  
   Pānesi       Parisato     se   Sahagaṇehi       Suriyobbhagaṇe       Vimbakapasuto hutvā       Tuṭṭhahaṭṭhaṃ ma se   Sihāsanaṃ ma      theragāthaṅkathāya vasadisaṃ apadānaṃ dissate iminā nāmena aññamapadānaṃ catupaññāsatime vagge vijjate 
  
                   
  
      Yāvatā devatā bhummā sabbe santipatuṃ tadā 
 Ratanāmayachattānaṃ vipākaṃ kathayissati 
  
      Tañca sabbaṃ suṇissāma kathayantassa satthuno 
 Bhiyyo bhāsaṃ janeyyāma sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Hemāsane nisīditvā sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghaparibbuḷho imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
      Yenidaṃ āsanaṃ dinnaṃ sovaṇṇaratanāmayaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Tiṃsa kappāni devindo devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Samantā yojanasataṃ ābhāyābhibhavissati 
  
      Manussalokaṃ āgantvā cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Pahassaroti nāmena uggatejo bhavissati 
  
      Divā vā yadi rattiṃ sataraṃsiva uggato 
 Samantā aṭṭharatanaṃ ujjetessati khattiyo 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
                  
  
      Tusitā hi cavitvāna sukkamūlena vodito 
 Kaccāno nāma nāmena brahmabandhu bhavissati 
  
      So pacchā pabbajitvāna arahā hessatanāsavo 
 Gotamo lokapajjoto aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati 
  
      Saṅkhittapucchitaṃ pañahaṃ vitthārena kathessati 
 Kathayanto ca taṃ pañahaṃ ajjhāsaṃ   purayissati  
  
      Aḍḍhe kule abhijato brāhmaṇo mantapāragu 
 Ohāya dhanadhaññāni pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
  
      Saṅkhittenapi pucchante vitthārena kathemahaṃ 
 Ajjhāsaṃ   tesaṃ puremi tosemi dipaduttamaṃ 
  
      Tosito me mahāvīro sayambhu aggapuggalo 
 Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākaccāno thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mahākaccānattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
   Ajjhāsayaṃ ma 
  
                   
  
    Kāḷudāyittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarabuddhassa   lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Addhānaṃ paṭipannassa carato cārikaṃ tadā 
  
      Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha uppalaṃ mallikañcahaṃ 
 Paramannaṃ gahetvāna adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
  
      Paribhuñaji mahāvīro paramannaṃ   subhojanaṃ 
 Tañca pupphaṃ gahetvāna janassa sampadassasī 
  
       Iṭṭhaṃ kantaṃ piyaṃ loke jalajaṃ pupphamuttamaṃ 
 Sudukkaraṃ tena kataṃ yo   me pupphaṃ adāsidaṃ   
  
                  
  
      Yo pupphamabhiropesi paramantañcadāsi me 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Dasa caṭṭhakkhattuṃ so   devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Uppalaṃ padumañcāpi mallikañca taduttari 
  
      Assa puññavipākena dibbagandhasamāyutaṃ 
 Ākāse chadanaṃ katvā dhārayissati tāvade 
  
      Pañcavisatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ pañcasataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma gottena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
      Sakakammābhiraddho so sukkamūlena codito 
 Sakyānaṃ nandijanano ñātibandhu bhavissati 
  
      So pacchā pabbajitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā canuppattaṃ katakiccamanāsavaṃ 
 Gotamo lokabandhu so etadagge ṭhapessati 
  
      Padhānapahitatto so upasanto nirūpadhi 
 Udāyi nāma nāmena hessati satthu sāvako  
  
      Rago doso ca moho ca   māno makkho ca dhaṃsito 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Tosayiñcāpi   sambuddhaṃ ātāpi nipako ahaṃ 
 Pamodito ca   sambuddho etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kāḷudāyī thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kaḷudāyittherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Pacadumattarassa     the se   Paripuṇṇa the   Yaṃ maṃ   Adāsi so se ma   Taṃ ma   Cittañca me suvimuttaṃ the       Tosayi tvāpi the   Pāsādikoca the 
  
                   
                  
  
    Mogharājattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Atthadassi tu bhagavā sayambhu aparājito 
 Bhikkhusaṅghaparibbuḷho rathiyaṃ paṭipajjatha 
  
      Sissehi samparivuto gharamhā abhinikkhamiṃ 
 Nikkhamitvānahaṃ tattha addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
      Abhivādiya   sambuddhaṃ sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
       Yāvatā rupino sattā arūpi vā asaññino 
 Sabbe te tava ñāṇambhi anto honti samogadhā   
  
      Sukhumacchikajālena udakaṃ yo parikkhipe 
 Ye keci udake pāṇā anto jāle bhavanti te 
  
      Yesañca cetanā atthi rūpino ca arūpino 
 Sabbe te tava ñāṇambhi anto honti samogadhā 
  
      Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ andhakārasamākulaṃ 
 Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna kaṅkāsotaṃ taranti te 
  
      Avijjānivuto loko andhakārena otthaṭo 
 Tava ñāṇambhi jotante andhakārā padhaṃsitā 
  
      Tuvaṃ cakkhusi sabbesaṃ mahātamapanudano 
 Tava dhammaṃ suṇitvāna nibbāyati bahujjano  
  
      Piṭharaṃ   purayitvāna madhukhuddaṃ   aneḷakaṃ 
 Ubhohatthehi paggayha upanesiṃ mahesino 
  
      Paṭigaṇhi mahāvīro sahatthena   mahāisi 
 Bhuñajitvā tañca sabbaññu vehāsaṃ nabhamuggami 
  
      Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā atthadassi narāsabho 
 Mama cittaṃ pasādento imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yenidaṃ thavitaṃ ñāṇaṃ buddhaseṭṭho ca thomito 
 Tena cittappasādena duggatiṃ so na gacchati 
  
      Catuddasakkhattuṃ so devajjaṃ karissati 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ   aṭṭhasataṃ   vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
  
   Abhivādetvāna       Samāhaṭā       Puṭakaṃ ma te   Buddamadhu the   Subhakena     se   Padesarajja     se   Davisataṃ the 
  
                   
                  
  
      Atha pañcasatakkhattuṃ   cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjamasaṅkheyyaṃ mahiyā kārayissati 
  
      Ajjhāyako mantadharo tiṇṇaṃ vedānapāragu 
 Gotamassa bhagavato sāsane pabbajissati 
  
      Gambhiraṃ tipuṇaṃ atthaṃ ñāṇena vicinissati 
 Mogharājāti nāmena hessati satthu sāmako 
  
      Tihi vijjāhi sampannaṃ katakiccaṃ anāsavaṃ   
 Gotamo satthavāhaggo etadagega ṭhapessati  
  
      Hitvā mānusakaṃ yogaṃ chetvāna bhavabandhanaṃ 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mogharājā thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Mogharājattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ   
  
    Adittattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi atthadassinaruttame 
 Upaṭṭhahiṃ   bhikkhusaṃghaṃ vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Nimantetvā saṅgharatanaṃ ujubhūtaṃ samāhitaṃ 
 Ucchunā maṇḍapaṃ katvā bhojesiṃ saṃghamuttamaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sabbe sate abhibhomi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭharase kappasete yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānami ucchudānassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā adhimutto thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Adhimuttattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
                  
  
    Lasuṇadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Himavantassa avidūre tāpaso āsahaṃ tadā 
 Lasuṇaṃ upajivāmi lasuṇaṃ mayha bhojanaṃ 
  
      Khāriyo purayitvāna saṃghārāmamagacchahaṃ 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena saṃghassa lasuṇaṃ adaṃ 
  
   Pañcave ma       Sampanenā katakicco anāsāvo     se  theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ dve therā iminā nāmena dissanti ayaṃ pana thero soḷasaṃnipāte dassito   Nimmantetvā     
  
                   
  
      Vipassissa naraggassa sāsane niratassahaṃ 
 Saṃghassa lasuṇaṃ datvā kappaṃ saggambhi modahaṃ 
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe lasuṇaṃ yamadaṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi lasuṇānaṃ   idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lasuṇadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Lasuṇadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
    Āyāgadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi sikhimbhi vadataṃ vare 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena avandiṃ thūpamuttamaṃ 
  
      Vaḍḍhakihi kathāpetvā mulaṃ datvānahaṃ tadā 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena āyāgaṃ kārapesahaṃ 
  
      Aṭṭha kappāni devesu abbocchinnaṃ vasiṃ ahaṃ 
 Avasesesu kappesu vokiṇṇaṃ saṃsariṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Kāye visaṃ na kamati sattāni na ca hanti me 
 Udakehaṃ na miyyāmi āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Yadicchāmi ahaṃ vassaṃ mahāmegho pavassati 
 Devāpi me vasaṃ enti puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattaratanasampanenā tiṃsakkhattuṃ ahosahaṃ 
 Na maṃ kecavajānanti puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
                  
  
      Ekatiṃse ito kappe āyāgaṃ yamakārayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āyāgassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āyāgadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Āyāgadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
    Dhammacakkikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato sihāsanassa sammukhā 
 Dhammacakkaṃ mayā ṭhapitaṃ sukataṃ viññuvaṇṇitaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Cāruvaṇṇova sobhāmi sayoggabalavāhano 
 Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ anuyuttā bahujjanā 
  
      Saṭṭhituriyasahassehi paricāremahaṃ   sadā 
 Parivārena sobhāmi puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ cakkaṃ ṭhapayiṃ ahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānimi dhammacakkassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ekādase kappe aṭṭhāsiṃsu  janādhipā 
 Sahassarājānāmena cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammacakkiko thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Dhammacakkikattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
    Kapparukkhiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavāto thupaseṭṭhassa sammukhā 
 Vicittadusse laggetvā   kapparukkhaṃ ṭhapesahaṃ 
  
      Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ 
 Sobhayanto mama dvāraṃ kapparūkkhopatiṭṭhati   
  
                  
  
      Ahañca parisā ceva ye keci mama nissitā    
 Tamhā dussaṃ gahetvāna nivāsema mayaṃ sadā 
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ rukkhaṃ ṭhapayiṃ   tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi kapparukkhassidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito ca sattamo kappe suceḷā aṭṭha khattiyā 
 Sattaratanasampannā cakkavatti mahabbālā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kapparukkhiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kapparukkhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Kuṇḍa   sāgata   kaccānā udāyī mogharājako 
 Adhimutto lasuṇado āyāgi   dhammacakkiko 
 Kapparukkhi ca dasamo gāthāyo dvādasa satanti 
   Kuṇḍadhānavaggo catuttho   
  
   Parivāremahaṃ       Laṅghitvā se       Patiṭṭhahi ma   Vāsikā se vasasitā ma   Capayiṃ se   Āsabha ma  aṭṭha āsuṃ  
  
                   
  
    Bhāgineyyaupālittherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Khiṇāsamasahassehi parivuto lokanāyako 
 Vivekamanuyutto so gacchate paṭisallituṃ 
  
      Ajitena nivatthohaṃ tidaṇḍaparidhārako   
 Bhikkhusaṃghaparibbuḷahaṃ addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
                  
  
      Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā sire katvāna añjaliṃ 
 Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
       Yathāṇḍajā ca saṃsedā opapāti jalābujā 
 Kākādipakkhino sabbe antaḷikkhavarā sadā   
  
      Ye keci pāṇabhūtatthi saññino vā asaññino 
 Sabbe te tava ñāṇambhi anto honti samogadhā 
  
      Gandhā ca pabbateyyā ye bhimavantanaguttame 
 Sabbe te tava silambhi kalāya   pi na yujjare 
  
      Mohandhakārapakkhanno ayaṃ loko sadevako 
 Tava ñāṇampi jotante andhakārā vidhaṃsitā 
  
      Yathā atthaṅgate suriye honti sattā tamogatā 
 Evaṃ buddho anuppanne hoti loko tamogato   
  
      Yathodayanto ādicco vinodeti tamaṃ sadā 
 Tatheva tvaṃ buddhaseṭṭha viddhaṃsesi tamaṃ sadā 
  
      Padhāpabhitattosi buddho loke sadevake 
 Tava kammābhiraddhena tosesi janataṃ bahuṃ  
  
      Taṃ sabbaṃ anumodivo padumuttaro mahāmuni 
 Nabhaṃ abbhuggami dhīro haṃsarājāva ambare 
  
      Abbhuggantvāna sambuddho mahesi padumuttaro 
 Antaḷikkhe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yadidaṃ thavitaṃ ñāṇaṃ opammehi samāyutaṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Aṭṭhārasakkhattuṃ so devarājā bhavissati 
 Pathavyā rajjaṃ tisataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
  
      Pañcavisatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ gaṇanāto asaṃkhiyaṃ 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi okkākakulasambhavo 
 Gotamo nāma nāmena satthā loke bhavissati 
  
   Dhāraṇe se parivāreṇo       Antaḷikkhe padesagā       Kālāyo se       Honti lokā tamogatā se 
  
                   
  
      Tusitā hi cavitvāna sukkamūlena codito 
 Bhinova jātiyā santo upāli nāma hessati 
  
                  
  
      So ca pacchā pabbajitvā virājetvāna pāpakaṃ 
 Sabbasave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo 
  
      Tuṭṭho ca gotamo buddho sakyaputto mahāyaso 
 Vinayādhigataṃ taṃ sa etadagge ṭhapessati  
  
      Saddhāyāhaṃ pabbajito katakicco anāsavo 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Bhagavā cānukampi maṃ vinayehaṃ visārado 
 Sakakammābhiraddho ca vihārāmi anāsavo 
  
      Saṃvuto pātimokkhambhi indriyesu ca pañcasu  
 Dhāremi vinayaṃ sabbaṃ kevalaṃ ratanākaraṃ 
  
      Mamañca guṇamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro 
 Bhikkhusajaṃghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upāli thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Bhāgineyyaupālittherassa   apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
    Soṇakoṭikaṇṇa  ttherāpadānaṃ 
  
       Anomadassimunino lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Sudhāya lepanaṃ katvā caṅkamaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Nānāvaṇṇehi pupphehi caṅkamaṃ santhariṃ ahaṃ 
 Ākāse vitānaṃ katvā bhojasiṃ buddhamuttamaṃ 
  
   Bhāgineyyaupālittherassa aṭṭhakathā  sihalakkharamuddita potthake  bhāgineyya  iti na dissate 
    Kuṭikaṇṇa  itipi pātho 
   Ito paṭṭhāya dissamānaṃ apadānaṃ soṇakeṃḷiyavessattherassāti sihalakkharamuddita apadānapāḷiyaṃ ca soṇakoḷivisattherassāni marammakkharamudditāpadānapāḷiyaṃ ca āgacchati Theragāthaṭṭhakathāyampi imā gāthā kolivisattheracarite nicesitā Apadānaṭṭhakathā cariyo pana apadānamidaṃ soṇakoṭikaṇṇattherassāni ca so thero koliyarājavajase jāno ti ca dassesi so panāyaṃ thero soṇo koḷiviso vā soṇo kuṭikaṇṇo vā bhavatu ayaṃ ambhākaṃ bhagavato sāsane etadaggaṭṭhānaṃ labhiti apadānapāḷiyā eva viññāyate Āraddhaviriyānaṃ aggataṃ gato soṇo kolivisatthero campānagare vessakule jāto ni ca kalyāṇavākkaraṇānaṃ aggaṭṭhānappatto koṭikaṇṇatthero avantijanapade kāḷiyā nama seṭṭhihariyāya kucchimbhi uppannoti ca mahāvaggapāḷi manorathapuraṇiādihi pāmāṇikehi gatthehi suvisadaṃ pākaṭi bhavati Apadānapāḷiyaṃ ekunacattāḷisatime vaggedisasamānaṃ soṇakoṭivisattherassa apadānaṃ pana manorathapuraṇiyā dassitena āraddhaviriyānaṃ aggataṃ gatassa soṇakoḷivisattherassa caritte saddhiṃ sameti Tasmāidaṃ      apadānaṃ apadānaṭṭhakathāyaṃ dissamānassa soṇassa koṭikaṇṇattherassevāti avagantabbaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Añajalimpaggahetvāna abhivādetvāna subbataṃ 
 Dighasālaṃ bhagavato niyyādesamahaṃ tadā 
  
      Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anutataro 
 Paṭiggahesi bhagavā anukampāya cakkhumā 
  
      Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho dakkhiṇeyyo sadevake 
 Bikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo so haṭṭhena cittena dighasālaṃ akāsi   me 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
                  
  
      Imassa maccukālambhi puññakammasamaṅgino 
 Sahassayuttassaratho upaṭṭhassati tāvade 
  
      Tena yānenayaṃ poso devalokaṃ gamissati 
 Anumodissare devā sampate kusale bhave 
  
      Mahārahaṃ vyamhaseṭṭhaṃ ratanamattikalepanaṃ  
 Kuṭāgāravarūpetaṃ vyambhaṃ ajjhavasissati 
  
      Tiṃsa kappasahassāni devaloke ramissati 
 Pañcavisati kappāni devarājā bhavissati 
  
      Sattasattatikkhattuñca cakkavatti bhavissati 
 Yasodhara sanāmā   te sabbepi ekanāmakā 
  
      Dve sampatti anubhotvā cinitvā  puññasañcayaṃ 
 Aṭṭhavisatikappambi cakkavatti bhavissati 
  
      Tatrāpi vyamhaṃ pavaraṃ vissakammena māpitaṃ 
 Dasasaddāvicittaṃ taṃ puramajjhivasissati 
  
      Aparimeyye ito kappe bhumipālo mahiddhiko  
 Okkāko nāma nāmena rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati 
  
      Soḷasitthisahassānaṃ sabbāsaṃ pavarā ca sā  
 Abhijātā khattiyāni tava putte janessati 
  
      Tava putte janetvāna khattiyāni marissati 
 Taruṇi ca piyā   aññā  mahesittaṃ karissati 
  
      Okkākaṃ tosayitvāna varaṃ kaññā   labhissati 
 Varaṃ laddhānaṃ   sā kaññā putte pabbajayissati 
  
      Pabbājitā ca te sabbe gamissanti taguttamaṃ 
 Jātibhedabhayā sabbe bhaginihi saṃvasissare   
  
      Ekā ca kaññā vyadhihi bhavissati parikkhatā    
 Mā no jāti pabhijja ti nikkhiṇissanti khattiyā 
  
      Khattiyo niharitvāna tāya saddhiṃ vasisasati 
 Bhavissati tadā bhedo okkākakulasambhavo 
  
   Adāsi the se machasaṃ   Ratanabhittisamujjalaṃ the   Samānā simu   Vaḍḍhetvā si mu   Yā the sāyā   Sāsiyā the  kaññā machasaṃ   Kaññaṃ the   Varaladadhā the   Vasissare machasaṃ        Purakkhatā     se syā 
  
                   
                  
  
      Tesaṃ pajā bhavissanti kolāyā nāma jātiyā 
 Tattha mānusakaṃ bhogaṃ anubossantanappakaṃ 
  
      Tamhā kāyā cavivona devalokaṃ gamissati 
 Tatrāpi pavaraṃ vyambhaṃ vindissati   manoramaṃ 
  
      Devalokā cavitvāna sukkamūlena codino 
 Āgantvāna manussattaṃ soṇo nāma bhavissati 
  
      Āraddhaviriyo pabhitatto padahaṃ satthu sāsane 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissanatāsavo 
  
      Anantadassi   bhagavā gotamo sakyapuṅgavo 
 Visesaññu mahāvīro aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapessati  
  
       
  
      Uttame damathe   danto cittaṃ me suppaṇihitaṃ 
 Bhāro me obhito sabbo nibbutomhi anāsavo 
  
      Aṃgiraso mahānāgo abhijātova kesarī 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇo koṭikaṇṇo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Soṇakoṭikaṇṇattherassa apadānaṃ dūtiyaṃ   
  
    Kāḷigodhāputtabhaddiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarasambuddhaṃ mettacittaṃ mahāmuniṃ 
 Upeti janatā sabbā sabbalokagganāyakaṃ 
  
      Vattha ṃsenāsanaṃ ceva   āmisaṃ pānabhojanaṃ 
 Dadanti satthuno sabbe puññakkhette anuttare 
  
                  
  
      Ahampi dānaṃ dassāmi devadevassa tādino 
 Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ nimantetvā saṃghampi ca anuttaraṃ 
  
      Uyyojitā mayā cete nimantesuṃ tathāgataṃ 
 Kevalaṃ bhikkhusaṅghañca puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ 
  
   Labhissati the machasaṃ   Atthadassi se the   vuṭṭhāmbhi deve caturaṅgulambhi   tiṇe anilerita aṅgaṇambhi ṭhātvāna yogassa payuttatādino   tatottariṃ pajaragatā na vijjati  dissate cāyaṃ gāthā maramma chaṭṭhasaṅgiti potthake Theragāthaṭṭhakathāyaṃ pana  vaṭṭambhi deve caturaṅgule patite anileritāpādapasampaghuṭṭhe jhane ratassappasussata tādino tato rati paramatarā na vijjati ti gāthā āgatā tathāpissā ḷuttha ucitanā natthi   Uttamena damathena te   Bhadadiyattherāpadānaṃ sī mu   Satatukañcabaddhakañca machasaṃ     padakaṃ se sattukañca pavākañca syā 
  
                   
  
      Satasahassa   pallaṅkaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ goṇakatthataṃ 
 Tulikā paṭalikāya   khomakappāsikehi   ca 
 Mahārahaṃ paññapesiṃ āsanaṃ buddhayuttakaṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu devadevo narāsabho 
 Bhikkhusaṃghaparibbuḷho mama dvāraṃ upāgami 
  
      Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ lokanāthaṃ yasassinaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumāno atināmayiṃ sakaṃ   gharaṃ 
  
      Bhikkhunaṃ satasahassaṃ buddañca lokanāyakaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano paramannena tappayiṃ 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā imā gāthā abhasatha 
  
       Yenidaṃ āsanaṃ dinnaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ goṇakatthataṃ 
 Tamahaṃ kittayisasāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Catusattatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Anubhossati sampattiṃ accharāhi purakkhato 
  
      Padesarajjaṃ sahassaṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
 Ekapaññasakkhattuñca cakakvatti bhavissati 
  
      Sabbāsu bhavayonisu uccākuli   bhavissati 
 So ca pacchā pabbajitvā sukkamūlena codito 
 Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena hessati satthusāvako  
  
      Vivekamanuyuttomhi pantasenanivāsahaṃ 
 Phalañcādhigataṃ sabbaṃ catta  kelayomhi ajajahaṃ 
  
      Mama sabbaṃ abhiññāya sababaññu lokanāyako 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe nisīditvā etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
                  
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhaddiyo kāḷigodhāya thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Kāḷigodhāputassa bhaddiyattherassa apadānaṃ tatiyaṃ   
  
   Sahassa     se   Paṭalikā ca the   Kappāsikepi the   Atināmayitaṃ the saṃgharaṃ machasaṃ   Kulinova the   Bhinna the 
  
                   
  
    Santiṭṭhāpakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Araññe kuṭikaṃ katvā vasāmi pabbatantare 
 Lābhālābhena santuṭṭho yasena ayasena ca 
  
      Padumuttaro lokavidu āhutitaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Visisatasahassehi āgacchi mama sanatikaṃ 
  
      Upāgataṃ mahāvīraṃ jalajuttaranāmakaṃ 
 Tiṇasattharaṃ paññapetvā adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ 
  
      Pasannacitto sumano āmaṇḍaṃ pāniyañcahaṃ 
 Adāsiṃ ujubhūtassa vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe   yaṃ dānadadiṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ekatāḷisakappambhi eko āsiṃ arindamo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sanniṭṭhāpako   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sanniṭapakattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
    Pañcahatthiyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Sumedho nāma sambuddho gacchate antarāpaṇe 
 Okkhittacakkhu   mitabhāṇi satimā saṃvutindriyo 
  
      Pañca uppalahatthāni āvalatthaṃ ahaṃsu   me 
 Tena buddhaṃ apūjesiṃ pasanto sehi pāṇihi 
  
                  
  
      Āropitā ca te pupphā chadanaṃ āsu   satthuno 
 Saṃsāviṃsu   mahānāgaṃ sissā ācariyaṃ yathā 
  
      Tiṃsakappasahassamhi yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānami buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Ito visakappasate ahesuṃ pañca khattiyā 
 Hatthiyā nāma nāmena cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pañcahatthiyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Pañcahattiyattherassa apadānaṃ catutthaṃ   
  
   Ito kappasatasahasse se   Sannidhāpako sī mu   Khitta cakkhu  sabbattha    Ācelatthamakāsi     se   Assa machasaṃ     se assu a   Samādhiṃsu machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
    Padumacchadaniyattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Nibbute lokanāthambhi vipassimhaggapuggalo 
 Suphullaṃ padumaṃ gayha citakamāropayiṃ ahaṃ   
  
      Āropite ca citake cehāsaṃ nabhamuggami 
 Ākāsacchadanaṃ katvā citakambhi adhārayiṃ   
  
      Ekanavute ito kappe yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Sattatāḷisito kappe padumissaranāmako 
 Cāturanto vijitāvi cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumacchadaniyo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Padumacchadaniyattherassa apadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ   
  
    Sayanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato mettacittassa tādino 
 Sayanaggaṃ mayā dinanaṃ dussabhaṇḍehi atthataṃ 
  
      Paṭiggahesi bhagavā kappiyaṃ sayanāsanaṃ 
 Uṭṭhāya āsanā tamhā vehāsaṃ uggami jino 
  
                  
  
      Catunavute ito kappe yaṃ sayanamadāsahaṃ 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi sayanadānassidaṃ   phalaṃ 
  
      Ekapaññāsito kappe varuṇo   devasavahayo 
 Sattaratanasampanno cakkavatti mahabbalo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sayanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ sattamaṃ   
  
    Caṅkamadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Atthadassa munino lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Iṭṭhakāhi cinitvāna caṅkamaṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ 
  
      Uccato pañcaratanaṃ caṅkamaṃ sādhu māpitaṃ 
 Āyāmato hatthasataṃ bhāvaniyaṃ   manoramaṃ 
  
      Paṭiggahesi bhagavā atthadassi naruttamo 
 Hatthena pulinaṃ gayha imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
   Tadā sīmu   Adhārayi sī mu   Sayanassa idaṃ machasaṃ   Carako machasaṃ   Bhāvaniyyaṃ machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
       Iminā pulinadānena caṅkamaṃ sukatena ca 
 Sattaratanasampannaṃ pulinaṃ anubhossati 
  
      Tīṇikappāni devesu devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Anubhossati sampattiṃ accharāhi purakkhato 
  
      Manussalokaṃ āgantvā rājā raṭṭhe bhavissati 
 Tikkhattuṃ cakkavatti ca mabhiyā so bhavissati  
  
      Aṭṭhārase kappasate yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā 
 Duggatiṃ nābhijānami caṅkamassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā caṅkama  dāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Caṅkamadāyakattherassa  apadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ   
  
                   
  
    Subhaddattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumutaro lokavidu āhutinaṃ paṭiggaho 
 Janataṃ uddharitvāna nibbāyati mahāyaso 
  
      Nibbāyante ca sambuddhe dasasahassī pakamapatha    
 Janakāyo mahā āsi devā sannipatuṃ 
  
      Vandanaṃ pūjayitthāna   nagara   mallikābhi ca 
 Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena ālepesiṃ   naruttamaṃ 
  
      Mama saṅkappamaññāya satthā loke anuttaro 
 Nipannakova sambuddho imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yo me pacchimake kāle gandhamālyena   chādayī 
 Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Ito cuto ayaṃ poso tusitakāyaṃ gamissati 
 Tattha rajjaṃ karitvanā nimmānaṃ so gamissati 
  
      Eteneva upāyena datvā malyaṃ   varuttamaṃ 
 Sakakammābhiraddho so sampattiṃ anubhossati 
  
      Punāpi tusite kāye nibbattisastayaṃ naro 
 Tamhā kāyā cavitvāna manussattaṃ gamissati 
  
      Sakyaputto mahānāgo aggo loke sadevake 
 Bodhayitvā bahu satte nibbāyissati cakkhumā 
  
   Caṅkamanā machasaṃ se   Dahasahasasikampatha machasaṃ   Purayitvāna sīmu machasaṃ   Tagarā machasaṃ   Aropesiṃ se syā āropayiṃ machasaṃ   Mālena machasaṃ mallena syā   Mālaṃ machasaṃ mallā syā  caṅkamanadāyakattherassa machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
      Pabbajjupagato   santo sukkamūlena codito 
 Upasaṅkamama sambuddhaṃ pañahaṃ pucchissati tadā 
  
      Hāsayitvāna   sambuddho sabbaññu lokanayako 
 Puññakammaṃ pariññāya saccāni vicarissati 
  
      Āraddho ca ayaṃ pañeha tuṭṭho ekaggamānaso 
 Satthāraṃ abhivādetvā pabbajjaṃ yāvayissati 
  
      Pasannamānasaṃ disvā sakkammena tositaṃ 
 Pabbājessati so buddho aggadhammassa kovido 
  
      Vāyamitvānayaṃ poso sammāsambuddhasāsane 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāvo  
  Pañcamahāṇavāraṃ   
  
                   
  
      Pubbakammena saṃyutto ekaggo susamābhito 
 Buddhassa oraso putto dhammajombhi sunimmito 
  
      Dhammarājaṃ upāgamma   āpucchiṃ pañahamuttamaṃ 
 Kathayanto ca me pañahaṃ dhammasotaṃ upānayī 
  
      Tassāhaṃ dhammamaññāya vihāsiṃ sāsane rato 
 Sabbāseve pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Satasahasse ito kappe jalajuttaranāyako 
 Nibbāyi anupādāno dipova telasaṅkhayā 
  
      Sattayojanikaṃ āsi thupañca ratanāmayaṃ 
 Dhajaṃ tattha apūjesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ manoramaṃ 
  
      Kassapassa ca buddhassa tisso nāmaggasāvako 
 Putto me oraso āsi dāyado jinasāsane 
  
      Tassa bhanena manasā vācaṃ bhāsiṃ abhaddakaṃ 
 Tena kammavipākena pacchime addasaṃ jinaṃ   
  
      Upavattane sālavane pacchime sayane muni 
 Pabbājesi mahāvīro hito kāruṇiko jino 
  
      Ajjevadāni pabbajā ajjeva upasampadā 
 Ajjeva parinibbāṇaṃ sammukhā dipaduttame 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā subhaddo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Subhaddattherassa apadānaṃ navamaṃ   
  
   Tadāsopagato sīmu machasaṃ   Bhāsayitvāna se       Upāgantvā       Pacchā me āsi bhaddakaṃ machasaṃ se 
  
                   
  
    Cundattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Siddhatthassa bhagavato lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Agghiyaṃ kārayitvāna jātipupphehi chādayi 
  
      Niṭṭhāpevona taṃ pupphaṃ buddhassa upanāmayiṃ 
 Pupphāvasesaṃ paggayha buddhassa abhiropayiṃ 
  
                   
  
      Kañcanagaghiyasaṅkāyaṃ buddhaṃ lokagganāyakaṃ 
 Pasannacitto sumano pupphagaghiyamupānayiṃ 
  
      Vitiṇṇakaṅkho sambuddho tiṇṇoghehi purakkhato 
 Bhikkhusaṃghi nisīdivo imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Dibbagandhaṃ pavāyantaṃ yo me pupphagghiyaṃ adā 
 Tamahaṃ nittayissāmi suṇātha mama bhāsato 
  
      Ito cuto ayaṃ peso devasaṃghapurakkhato 
 Jātipupphehi parikiṇṇo devalokaṃ gamissati 
  
      Ubbiddhaṃ bhagavanaṃ tassa sovaṇṇañca maṇimayaṃ 
 Vyamhaṃ pātubhavissati puññakammappabhāvitaṃ 
  
      Catusattatikkhattuṃ so devarajjaṃ karissati 
 Anubhossati sampattiṃ accharāhi purakkhato 
  
      Pathavyā rajjaṃ tisataṃ vasudhaṃ āvasissati 
 Pañcasattanikkhattuñca accharābhi purakkhato 
  
      Dujjayo nāma nāmena hessati manujādhipo 
 Anubhotvāna taṃ puññaṃ sakakammaṃ apassito 
  
      Vinipātaṃ aganvāna   manussattaṃ gamissati 
 Hiraññassa ca nicitaṃ koṭisatamanappakaṃ 
  
      Nibbattissati yonimbhi   brāhmaṇe   so bhavissati 
 Vaṅgattassa suto sāriyā oraso piyo 
  
      So ca pacchā pabbatvā aṅgirasassa sāsane 
 Culavundoti nāmena hessati satthu sāvako 
  
      Sāmaṇerova so santo khiṇāsavo bhavissati 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya nibbāyissatanāsavo  
  
      Upaṭṭhahiṃ mahāvīraṃ aññe ca pesale bahu 
 Bhātaraṃ ce cupaṭṭhāsiṃ uttamatthassa pattiyā 
  
      Bhātaraṃ me upaṭṭhitvā dhātu pattambhi opiya 
 Sambuddhaṃ upanāmesiṃ lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
  
   Āgantvā       Lokambhi       Brāhmaṇo machasaṃ     
  
                   
                   
  
      Ubho hatthehi paggayha buddho loke sadevake 
 Saṃdassayanto taṃ dhātuṃ kittayī aggasāvakaṃ 
  
      Cittaṃ ca suvimuttaṃ me saddhā mayhaṃ patiṭṭhitā 
 Sabbāsave pariññāya viharāmi anāsavo 
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca phassito 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā cundo thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Cundattherassa apadānaṃ dasamaṃ   
  
 Uddānaṃ 
 Upāli soṇo bhaddiyo santiṭṭhāpaka   hatthiyo 
 Gāthā sataṃ ca tāḷisaṃ catasso ca taduttari 
   Upālivaggo pañcamo 
  
    Vidhupanāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarabuddhassa lokajeṭṭhassa tādino 
 Vijanikā   mayā dinnā didapadindassa tādino 
  
      Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā paggahetvāna añjaliṃ 
 Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho 
  
      Vijaniṃ paggahetvāna satthā loke anuttaro    
 Bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito santo imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha 
  
       Iminā vijanidānena cittassa paṇidhihi ca 
 Kappānaṃ satasahassaṃ vinipātaṃ na gacchati  
  
      Āraddhaviriyo pahitatto cetoguṇasamāhito 
 Jātiyā pattavassohaṃ arahattamapāpuṇiṃ 
  
      Saṭṭhakappasahassambhi vijamānasanāmakā  
 Soḷasāsiṃsu rājāno cakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vidhupanadāyako thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Vidhupanadāyakattherassa apadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ   
  
   Sannidhāpaka se   Bijanikā machasaṃ   Santhā lokagganāyako machasaṃ 
   Vijanāmasamānakā se bijamānasanāmakā machasaṃ 
  
                   
  
    Sataraṃsikattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Ucciyaṃ   selamāruya nisīdi purisuttamo 
 Pabbatassāvidurambhi brāhmaṇo mantapāragu 
  
      Upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāvīraṃ devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ 
 Añajalimpaggahetvāna satthaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ 
  
       Esa buddho mahāvīro varadhammappakāsako 
 Jalani aggikhandhova bhikkhusaṃghapurakkhato 
  
      Mahāsamuddo vakkhobho aṇṇavova duruttaro 
 Migarājāvasambhito dhammaṃ deseti cakkhumā  
  
      Mama saṅkappamaññāya padumuttaranāyako 
 Bhikkhusaṃghe ṭhito satthā imā gāthā abhāsatha 
  
       Yenāyaṃ añajali dinno buddhāseṭṭho ca thomitato 
 Tiṃsakappasahassāni devarajjaṃ karissati 
  
      Kappasatasahassambhi aṃgirasasanāmako 
 Vivattacchaddo   sambuddho uppajjissati tāvade 
  
      Tassa dhammesu dāyado oraso dhammanimmito  
 Sataraṃsiti nāmena arahā so bhavissati  
  
      Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ 
 Sataraṃsimbhi nāmena pabhā niddhāvate mama 
  
      Maṇḍape rukkhamule vā jhāyī jhānarato ahaṃ 
 Dhāremi antimaṃ dehaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsane 
  
      Saṭṭhikappasahassambhi caturo rāma   nāmakā 
 Sattaratanasampannā vakkavatti mahabbalā 
  
                   
  
      Paṭisambhidā catasse ca vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime 
 Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ 
  
 Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sataraṃsiyo   thero imā gathāyo abhāsitthāti 
   Sataraṃsikattherassa apadānaṃ dutiyaṃ   
  
    Sayanadāyakattherāpadānaṃ 
  
      Padumuttarabuddhassa sabbalokānukampino 
 Sayanaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ vippasannena cetasā 
  
      Tena sayanadānena sukhette bijasampadā 
 Bhogā nibbattare   tassa sayanassa idaṃ phalaṃ 
  
   Ubbiddhaṃ machasaṃ   Vicittachando machasaṃ se   Roma     se   Sataraṃsi machasaṃ   Bhogo nibbattate     se
